<li><a href="/wiki/Jesus_(name)" title="Jesus (name)">Jesus</a>, <i>savior; deliverer,</i><sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140"><span>[</span>140<span>]</span></a></sup> The Greek form of the name Joshua or Jeshua, a contraction of Jehoshua, that is, <i>help of Jehovah</i> or <i>saviour.</i><sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141"><span>[</span>141<span>]</span></a></sup> Latin: Jesus, Iesus, Iesu, Josue. Greek: Ieous from Hebrew Yeshua. Also means <i>safety, victory</i> and <i>who's help is Jehovah</i> or it may be from the verb "Yasha", "to save," and = Jehovah Savior, or simply Savior;<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142"><span>[</span>142<span>]</span></a></sup> a late form of Hebrew "yehosua", the meaning of which is "YHWH is salvation" or "YHWH saves/has saved." <sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143"><span>[</span>143<span>]</span></a></sup> Online definition of "savior." <sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144"><span>[</span>144<span>]</span></a></sup> Latin term drove out Old English "hland" which means "healer" as the preferred descriptive term for Jesus.<sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145"><span>[</span>145<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
